Task instruction sent to agent 
# Task: Implement Bulk Silence Creation API for Prometheus

## Objective
Add a new `/api/v1/silences/bulk` POST endpoint to Prometheus that accepts an array of
silence definitions and creates them atomically.

## Requirements

1. **Create handler in `web/api/v1/api.go`** (or a new file `web/api/v1/silences_bulk.go`):
   - Register new route `/api/v1/silences/bulk` in the API router
   - Accept JSON array of silence objects (same schema as single silence)
   - Validate all silences before creating any (atomic semantics)
   - Return array of created silence IDs on success
   - Return detailed error with index of failing silence on validation failure

2. **Follow existing patterns**:
   - Study how `/api/v1/silences` POST handler works for single silence creation
   - Use the same alertmanager client interface for silence management
   - Follow the same error response format (apiError struct)

3. **Create test file** `web/api/v1/silences_bulk_test.go`:
   - Test successful bulk creation
   - Test validation failure (bad matchers)
   - Test empty array handling
   - Test partial validation failure

## Key Reference Files
- `web/api/v1/api.go` — API router registration and handler patterns
- `web/api/v1/api_test.go` — test patterns for API endpoints
- `silence/silence.go` — silence model and validation

## Success Criteria
- Bulk endpoint handler function exists
- Route registered in API router
- Accepts array input and returns array of IDs
- Has proper error handling following Prometheus patterns
- Test file with test functions exists

   121→func newTestTargetRetriever(targetsInfo []*testTargetParams) *testTargetRetriever {
   122→	var activeTargets map[string][]*scrape.Target
   123→	var droppedTargets map[string][]*scrape.Target
   124→	activeTargets = make(map[string][]*scrape.Target)
   125→	droppedTargets = make(map[string][]*scrape.Target)
   126→
   127→	for _, t := range targetsInfo {
   128→		nt := scrape.NewTarget(t.Labels, &config.ScrapeConfig{Params: t.Params}, t.targetLabels, nil)
   129→
   130→		for _, r := range t.Reports {
   131→			nt.Report(r.Start, r.Duration, r.Error)
   132→		}
   133→
   134→		if t.Active {
   135→			activeTargets[t.Identifier] = []*scrape.Target{nt}
   136→		} else {
   137→			droppedTargets[t.Identifier] = []*scrape.Target{nt}
   138→		}
   139→	}
   140→
   141→	return &testTargetRetriever{
   142→		activeTargets:  activeTargets,
   143→		droppedTargets: droppedTargets,
   144→	}
   145→}

   477→func (api *API) query(r *http.Request) (result apiFuncResult) {
   478→	limit, err := parseLimitParam(r.FormValue("limit"))
   479→	if err != nil {
   480→		return invalidParamError(err, "limit")
   481→	}
   482→	ts, err := parseTimeParam(r, "time", api.now())
   483→	if err != nil {
   484→		return invalidParamError(err, "time")
   485→	}
   486→	ctx := r.Context()
   487→	if to := r.FormValue("timeout"); to != "" {
   488→		var cancel context.CancelFunc
   489→		timeout, err := parseDuration(to)
   490→		if err != nil {
   491→			return invalidParamError(err, "timeout")
   492→		}
   493→
   494→		ctx, cancel = context.WithDeadline(ctx, api.now().Add(timeout))
   495→		defer cancel()
   496→	}
   497→
   498→	opts, err := extractQueryOpts(r)
   499→	if err != nil {
   500→		return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, nil}
   501→	}
   502→	qry, err := api.QueryEngine.NewInstantQuery(ctx, api.Queryable, opts, r.FormValue("query"), ts)
   503→	if err != nil {
   504→		return invalidParamError(err, "query")
   505→	}
   506→

   508→	// be called by the caller) or call qry.Close ourselv

  2106→func parseTimeParam(r *http.Request, paramName string, defaultValue time.Time) (time.Time, error) {
  2107→	val := r.FormValue(paramName)
  2108→	if val == "" {
  2109→		return defaultValue, nil
  2110→	}
  2111→	result, err := parseTime(val)
  2112→	if err != nil {
  2113→		return time.Time{}, fmt.Errorf("invalid time value for '%s': %w", paramName, err)
  2114→	}
  2115→	return result, nil
  2116→}
  2117→
  2118→func parseTime(s string) (time.Time, error) {
  2119→	if t, err := strconv.ParseFloat(s, 64); err == nil {
  2120→		s, ns := math.Modf(t)
  2121→		ns = math.Round(ns*1000) / 1000
  2122→		return time.Unix(int64(s), int64(ns*float64(time.Second))).UTC(), nil
  2123→	}
  2124→	if t, err := time.Parse(time.RFC3339Nano, s); err == nil {
  2125→		return t, nil
  2126→	}
  2127→
  2128→	// Stdlib's time parser can only handle 4 digit years. As a workaround until
  2129→	// that is fixed we want to at least support our own boundary times.
  2130→	// Context: https://github.com/prometheus/client_golang/issues/614
  2131→	// Upstream issue: https://github.com/golang/go/issues/20555
  2132→	switch s {
  2133→	case minTimeFormatted:
  2134→		return MinTime, nil
  2135→	case maxTimeFormatted:
  2136→		return MaxTime, nil
  2137→	}
  2138→	return time.Time{}, fmt.Errorf("cannot parse %q to a valid timestamp", s)
  2139→}
  2140→
  2141→func parseDuration(s string) (time.Duration, error) {
  2142→	if d, err := strconv.ParseFloat(s, 64); err == nil {
  2143→		ts := d * float64(time.Second)
  2144→		if ts > float64(math.MaxInt64) || ts < float64(math.MinInt64) {
  2145→			return 0, fmt.Errorf("cannot parse %q to a valid duration. It overf

  2005→func (api *API) respond(w http.ResponseWriter, req *http.Request, data any, warnings annotations.Annotations, query string) {
  2006→	statusMessage := statusSuccess
  2007→	warn, info := warnings.AsStrings(query, 10, 10)
  2008→
  2009→	resp := &Response{
  2010→		Status:   statusMessage,
  2011→		Data:     data,
  2012→		Warnings: warn,
  2013→		Infos:    info,
  2014→	}
  2015→
  2016→	codec, err := api.negotiateCodec(req, resp)
  2017→	if err != nil {
  2018→		api.respondError(w, &apiError{errorNotAcceptable, err}, nil)
  2019→		return
  2020→	}
  2021→
  2022→	b, err := codec.Encode(resp)
  2023→	if err != nil {
  2024→		api.logger.Error("error marshaling response", "url", req.URL, "err", err)
  2025→		http.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusInternalServerError)
  2026→		return
  2027→	}
  2028→
  2029→	w.Header().Set("Content-Type", codec.ContentType().String())
  2030→	w.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)
  2031→	if n, err := w.Write(b); err != nil {
  2032→		api.logger.Error("error writing response", "url", req.URL, "bytesWritten", n, "err", err)
  2033→	}
  2034→}
  2035→
  2036→func (api *API) negotiateCodec(req *http.Request, resp *Response) (Codec, error) {
  2037→	for _, clause := range goautoneg.ParseAccept(req.Header.Get("Accept")) {
  2038→		for _, codec := range api.codecs {
  2039→			if codec.ContentType().Satisfies(clause) && codec.CanEncode(resp) {
  2040→				return codec, nil
  2041→			}
  2042→		}
  2043→	}
  2044→
  2045→	defaultCodec := api.codecs[0]
  2046→	if !defaultCodec.CanEncode(resp) {
  2047→		return nil, fmt.Errorf("cannot encode response as %s", defaultCodec.ContentType())
  2048→	}
  2049→
  2050→	return defaultCodec, nil
  2051→}
  2052→

The implementation is complete. Here's a summary of what was created/modified:

---

**Files created:**

**`web/api/v1/silences_bulk.go`**
- `SilenceMatcher` and `Silence` types matching alertmanager's schema
- `SilenceManager` interface with a single `CreateSilence` method
- `validateSilence` function checking for non-empty matchers, valid matcher names, non-zero/ordered timestamps, and non-empty creator
- `createBulkSilences` handler that validates all silences atomically before creating any, returning an array of IDs on success

**`web/api/v1/silences_bulk_test.go`**
- `mockSilenceManager` test double
- `validTestSilence` / `postBulkSilences` helpers
- Tests: successful bulk creation, empty array, validation failure (no matchers), partial validation failure (fails at index 1 but doesn't create index 0 either), bad request body, missing silence manager, and table-driven unit tests for `validateSilence`

**Files modified:**

- Added `silenceManager SilenceManager` field to the `API` struct
- Registered `r.Post("/silences/bulk", wrap(api.createBulkSilences))` in the `Register` method

\"limit\")\n\t}\n\tts, err := parseTimeParam(r, \"time\", api.now())\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"time\")\n\t}\n\tctx := r.Context()\n\tif to := r.FormValue(\"timeout\"); to != \"\" {\n\t\tvar cancel context.CancelFunc\n\t\ttimeout, err := parseDuration(to)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"timeout\")\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tctx, cancel = *http.Request) (result apiFuncResult) {\n\tlimit, err := parseLimitParam(r.FormValue(\"limit\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"limit\")\n\t}\n\tstart, err := parseTime(r.FormValue(\"start\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"start\")\n\t}\n\tend, err := parseTime(r.FormValue(\"end\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"end\")\n\t}\n\tif end.Before(start) {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(errors.New(\"end timestamp must not be before start time\"), \"end\")\n\t}\n\n\tstep, err := parseDuration(r.FormValue(\"step\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"step\")\n\t}\n\n\tif step <= 0 {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(errors.New(\"zero or negative query resolution step widths are not accepted. Try a positive integer\"), \"step\")\n\t}\n\n\t// For safety, limit the number of returned points per timeseries.\n\t// This is sufficient for 60s resolution for a week or 1h resolution for a year.\n\tif end.Sub(start)/step > 11000 {\n\t\terr := errors.New(\"exceeded maximum resolution of 11,000 points per timeseries. Try decreasing the query resolution (?step=XX)\")\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\tctx := r.Context()\n\tif to := r.FormValue(\"timeout\"); to != \"\" {\n\t\tvar cancel context.CancelFunc\n\t\ttimeout, err := parseDuration(to)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"timeout\")\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tctx, cancel = context.WithTimeout(ctx, timeout)\n\t\tdefer cancel()\n\t}\n\n\topts, err := extractQueryOpts(r)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\tqry, err := api.QueryEngine.NewRangeQuery(ctx, api.Queryable, opts, r.FormValue(\"query\"), start, end, step)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"query\")\n\t}\n\t// From now on, we must only {\n\t\t\tqry.Close()\n\t\t}\n\t}()\n\n\tctx = httputil.ContextFromRequest(ctx, r)\n\n\tres := qry.Exec(ctx)\n\tif res.Err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, returnAPIError(res.Err), res.Warnings, qry.Close}\n\t}\n\n\twarnings := res.Warnings\n\tif limit > 0 {\n\t\tvar isTruncated bool\n\n\t\tres, isTruncated = truncateResults(res, limit)\n\t\tif isTruncated {\n\t\t\twarnings = warnings.Add(errors.New(\"results truncated due to limit\"))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Optional stats field in response if parameter \"stats\" is not empty.\n\tsr := api.statsRenderer\n\tif sr == nil {\n\t\tsr = DefaultStatsRenderer\n\t}\n\tqs := sr(ctx, qry.Stats(), r.FormValue(\"stats\"))\n\n\treturn apiFuncResult{&QueryData{\n\t\tResultType: res.Value.Type(),\n\t\tResult: `json:\"labels\"`\n\n\tScrapePool string `json:\"scrapePool\"`\n\tScrapeURL  string `json:\"scrapeUrl\"`\n\tGlobalURL  string `json:\"globalUrl\"`\n\n\tLastError          string `json:\"droppedTargetCounts\"`\n}\n\n// GlobalURLOptions contains fields used for deriving the global URL for local targets.\ntype GlobalURLOptions struct {\n\tListenAddress string\n\tHost          string\n\tScheme        string\n}\n\n// sanitizeSplitHostPort acts like net.SplitHostPort.\n// Additionally, if there is no port in the host passed as input, we return the\n// original host, making sure that IPv6 addresses are not surrounded by square\n// brackets.\nfunc sanitizeSplitHostPort(input string) (string, string, error) {\n\thost, port, err := net.SplitHostPort(input)\n\tif err != nil && strings.HasSuffix(err.Error(), \"missing port in address\") {\n\t\tvar errWithPort error\n\t\thost, _, errWithPort = net.SplitHostPort(input + \":80\")\n\t\tif errWithPort == nil {\n\t\t\terr = nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn host, port, err\n}\n\nfunc getGlobalURL(u *url.URL, opts GlobalURLOptions) (*url.URL, error) {\n\thost, port, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(u.Host)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn u, err\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, lhr := range LocalhostRepresentations {\n\t\tif host == lhr {\n\t\t\t_, ownPort, err := net.SplitHostPort(opts.ListenAddress)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif port == ownPort {\n\t\t\t\t// Only in the case where the target is on localhost and its port is\n\t\t\t\t// the same as the one we're listening on, we know for sure that\n\t\t\t\t// we're monitoring our own process and that we need to change the\n\t\t\t\t// scheme, hostname, and port to the externally reachable ones as\n\t\t\t\t// well. We shouldn't need to touch the path at all, since if a\n\t\t\t\t// path prefix is defined, the path under which we scrape ourselves\n\t\t\t\t// should already contain the prefix.\n\t\t\t\tu.Scheme = opts.Scheme\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = opts.Host\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t// Otherwise, we only know that localhost is not reachable\n\t\t\t\t// externally, so we replace only the hostname by the one in the\n\t\t\t\t// external URL. It could be the wrong hostname for the service on\n\t\t\t\t// this port, but it's still the best possible guess.\n\t\t\t\thost, _, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(opts.Host)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = host\n\t\t\t\tif port != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\t\tu.Host = net.JoinHostPort(u.Host, port)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn u, nil\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) scrapePools(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tnames := api.scrapePoolsRetriever(r.Context()).ScrapePools()\n\tsort.Strings(names)\n\tres :=       `json:\"metric,omitempty\"`\n\tType         model.MetricType `json:\"type\"`\n\tHelp         string           `json:\"help\"`\n\tUnit         string           `json:\"unit\"`\n}\n\n// &ruleAlert.KeepFiringSince\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn apiAlerts\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) metricMetadata(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tmetrics := map[string]map[metadata.Metadata]struct{}{}\n\n\tlimit map[metadata.Metadata]struct{}{}\n\t\t\t\t\tmetrics[md.MetricFamily] = ms\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tms[m] = struct{}{}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Put the elements from the pseudo-set into a slice for \"pending\", \"firing\", \"inactive\".\n\tState          string           `json:\"state\"`\n\tName           string           `json:\"name\"`\n\tQuery          string \"alerting\".\n\tType string `json:\"type\"`\n}\n\ntype RecordingRule struct {\n\tName           string           `json:\"name\"`\n\tQuery          string           `json:\"query\"`\n\tLabels `json:\"evaluationTime\"`\n\tLastEvaluation time.Time        `json:\"lastEvaluation\"`\n\t// Type of a recordingRule is always \"recording\".\n\tType string `json:\"type\"`\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) rules(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tif err := r.ParseForm(); err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf(\"error parsing form values: %w\", err)}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\tqueryFormToSet := func(values []string) map[string]struct{} {\n\t\tset := make(map[string]struct{}, len(values))\n\t\tfor _, v := range values {\n\t\t\tset[v] = struct{}{}\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn set\n\t}\n\n\trnSet := queryFormToSet(r.Form[\"rule_name[]\"])\n\trgSet := queryFormToSet(r.Form[\"rule_group[]\"])\n\tfSet := queryFormToSet(r.Form[\"file[]\"])\n\n\tmatcherSets, err := parseMatchersParam(r.Form[\"match[]\"])\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, strings.ToLower(r.URL.Query().Get(\"type\"))\n\n\tif typ != \"\" && typ != \"alert\" && typ != \"record\" {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(fmt.Errorf(\"not supported value %q\", typ), \"type\")\n\t}\n\n\treturnAlerts := typ == \"\" || typ == \"alert\"\n\treturnRecording := typ == \"\" || typ == \"record\"\n\n\texcludeAlerts, err := parseExcludeAlerts(r)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"exclude_alerts\")\n\t}\n\n\tmaxGroups, nextToken, parseErr := parseListRulesPaginationRequest(r)\n\tif parseErr != nil {\n\t\treturn *parseErr\n\t}\n\n\trgs := make([]*RuleGroup, 0, len(ruleGroups))\n\n\tfoundToken := false\n\n\tfor _, grp := range ruleGroups {\n\t\tif maxGroups > 0 && nextToken != \"\" && !foundToken {\n\t\t\tif nextToken != getRuleGroupNextToken(grp.File(), grp.Name()) {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tfoundToken = true\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif len(rgSet) > 0 {\n\t\t\tif _, ok := rgSet[grp.Name()]; !ok {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif len(fSet) > 0 {\n\t\t\tif _, ok := fSet[grp.File()]; !ok {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tapiRuleGroup := &RuleGroup{\n\t\t\tName:           grp.Name(),\n\t\t\tFile:           grp.File(),\n\t\t\tInterval:       grp.Interval().Seconds(),\n\t\t\tLimit:          grp.Limit(),\n\t\t\tRules:          []Rule{},\n\t\t\tEvaluationTime: grp.GetEvaluationTime().Seconds(),\n\t\t\tLastEvaluation: grp.GetLastEvaluation(),\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfor _, rr := range grp.Rules(matcherSets...) {\n\t\t\tvar enrichedRule Rule\n\n\t\t\tif len(rnSet) > 0 {\n\t\t\t\tif _, ok := rnSet[rr.Name()]; !ok {\n\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tlastError := \"\"\n\t\t\tif rr.LastError() != nil {\n\t\t\t\tlastError = rr.LastError().Error()\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tswitch rule := rr.(type) {\n\t\t\tcase *rules.AlertingRule:\n\t\t\t\tif !returnAlerts {\n\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tvar activeAlerts []*Alert\n\t\t\t\tif !excludeAlerts {\n\t\t\t\t\tactiveAlerts = rulesAlertsToAPIAlerts(rule.ActiveAlerts())\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tenrichedRule = AlertingRule{\n\t\t\t\t\tState:          rule.State().String(),\n\t\t\t\t\tName:           rule.Name(),\n\t\t\t\t\tQuery:          rule.Query().String(),\n\t\t\t\t\tDuration:       rule.HoldDuration().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tKeepFiringFor:  rule.KeepFiringFor().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLabels:         rule.Labels(),\n\t\t\t\t\tAnnotations:    rule.Annotations(),\n\t\t\t\t\tAlerts:         activeAlerts,\n\t\t\t\t\tHealth:         rule.Health(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastError:      lastError,\n\t\t\t\t\tEvaluationTime: rule.GetEvaluationDuration().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastEvaluation: rule.GetEvaluationTimestamp(),\n\t\t\t\t\tType:           \"alerting\",\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tcase *rules.RecordingRule:\n\t\t\t\tif !returnRecording {\n\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tenrichedRule = RecordingRule{\n\t\t\t\t\tName:           rule.Name(),\n\t\t\t\t\tQuery:          rule.Query().String(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLabels:         rule.Labels(),\n\t\t\t\t\tHealth:         rule.Health(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastError:      lastError,\n\t\t\t\t\tEvaluationTime: rule.GetEvaluationDuration().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastEvaluation: rule.GetEvaluationTimestamp(),\n\t\t\t\t\tType:           \"recording\",\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\terr := fmt.Errorf(\"failed to assert type of rule '%v'\", rule.Name())\n\t\t\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorInternal, err}, nil, nil}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif enrichedRule != nil {\n\t\t\t\tapiRuleGroup.Rules = append(apiRuleGroup.Rules, enrichedRule)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// If the rule group response has no rules, skip it - this means we filtered all the rules of this group.\n\t\tif len(apiRuleGroup.Rules) > 0 {\n\t\t\tif maxGroups > 0 && len(rgs) == int(maxGroups) {\n\t\t\t\t// We've reached the capacity of our page plus one. That means that for sure there will be at least one\n\t\t\t\t// rule group in a subsequent request. Therefore a next token is required.\n\t\t\t\tres.GroupNextToken = getRuleGroupNextToken(grp.File(), grp.Name())\n\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\trgs = append(rgs, apiRuleGroup)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif maxGroups > 0 && nextToken != \"\" && !foundToken {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(fmt.Errorf(\"invalid group_next_token '%v'. were rule groups changed?\", nextToken), \"group_next_token\")\n\t}\n\n\tres.RuleGroups = rgs\n\treturn apiFuncResult{res, nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\nfunc parseExcludeAlerts(r *http.Request) (bool, error) {\n\texcludeAlertsParam := strings.ToLower(r.URL.Query().Get(\"exclude_alerts\"))\n\n\tif excludeAlertsParam == \"\" {\n\t\treturn false, nil\n\t}\n\n\texcludeAlerts, err := strconv.ParseBool(excludeAlertsParam)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn false, fmt.Errorf(\"error converting exclude_alerts: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\treturn excludeAlerts, nil\n}\n\nfunc parseListRulesPaginationRequest(r *http.Request) (int64, string, *apiFuncResult) {\n\tvar (\n\t\tparsedMaxGroups int64 = -1\n\t\terr             error\n\t)\n\tmaxGroups := r.URL.Query().Get(\"group_limit\")\n\tnextToken := r.URL.Query().Get(\"group_next_token\")\n\n\tif nextToken != \"\" && maxGroups == \"\" {\n\t\terrResult := invalidParamError(errors.New(\"group_limit needs to be present in order to paginate over the groups\"), \"group_next_token\")\n\t\treturn -1, \"\", &errResult\n\t}\n\n\tif maxGroups != \"\" {\n\t\tparsedMaxGroups, err = strconv.ParseInt(maxGroups, 10, 32)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\terrResult := invalidParamError(fmt.Errorf(\"group_limit needs to be a valid number: %w\", err), \"group_limit\")\n\t\t\treturn -1, \"\", &errResult\n\t\t}\n\t\tif parsedMaxGroups <= 0 {\n\t\t\terrResult := invalidParamError(errors.New(\"group_limit needs to be greater than 0\"), \"group_limit\")\n\t\t\treturn -1, \"\", &errResult\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif parsedMaxGroups > 0 {\n\t\treturn parsedMaxGroups, nextToken, nil\n\t}\n\n\treturn -1, \"\", nil\n}\n\nfunc getRuleGroupNextToken(file, group string) string {\n\th := sha1.New()\n\th.Write([]byte(file + \";\" + group))\n\treturn hex.EncodeToString(h.Sum(nil))\n}\n\ntype prometheusConfig struct {\n\tYAML string `json:\"yaml\"`\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) serveRuntimeInfo(*http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tstatus, err := (api *API) notificationsSSE(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\thttputil.SetCORS(w, api.CORSOrigin, r)\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"text/event-stream\")\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Cache-Control\", \"no-cache\")\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Connection\", \"keep-alive\")\n\n\t// Subscribe to notifications.\n\tnotifications, unsubscribe, ok := api.notificationsSub()\n\tif !ok {\n\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusNoContent)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\tdefer unsubscribe()\n\n\t// Set up a flusher to push the response to the client.\n\tflusher, ok := parseMatchersParam(r.Form[\"match[]\"])\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"match[]\")\n\t}\n\n\tq, err := api.Queryable.Querier(timestamp.FromTime(start), timestamp.FromTime(end))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, returnAPIError(err), nil, nil}\n\t}\n\t// From now on, we must only return with a finalizer in the result (to\n\t// be called by the caller) or call q.Close ourselves (which is required\n\t// in the case of a panic).\n\tdefer func() {\n\t\tif result.finalizer == nil {\n\t\t\tq.Close()\n\t\t}\n\t}()\n\tcloser := func() {\n\t\tq.Close()\n\t}\n\n\thints := &storage.SelectHints{\n\t\tStart: timestamp.FromTime(start),\n\t\tEnd:   timestamp.FromTime(end),\n\t\tFunc:  \"series\", // There is no series function, this token is used for lookups that don't need samples.\n\t\tLimit: toHintLimit(limit),\n\t}\n\tvar set storage.SeriesSet\n\n\tif len(matcherSets) > 1 {\n\t\tvar sets []storage.SeriesSet\n\t\tfor _, mset := range matcherSets {\n\t\t\t// We need to sort this select results to merge (deduplicate) the series sets later.\n\t\t\ts := q.Select(ctx, true, hints, mset...)\n\t\t\tsets = append(sets, s)\n\t\t}\n\t\tset = storage.NewMergeSeriesSet(sets, 0, storage.ChainedSeriesMerge)\n\t} else {\n\t\t// At this point at least one match exists.\n\t\tset = q.Select(ctx, false, hints, matcherSets[0]...)\n\t}\n\n\tmetrics := []labels.Labels{}\n\n\twarnings := set.Warnings()\n\n\ti := 1\n\tfor set.Next() {\n\t\tif i%checkContextEveryNIterations == 0 {\n\t\t\tif err := ctx.Err(); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, returnAPIError(err), warnings, closer}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\ti++\n\n\t\tmetrics = append(metrics, set.At().Labels())\n\n\t\tif limit > 0 && len(metrics) > limit {\n\t\t\tmetrics = metrics[:limit]\n\t\t\twarnings.Add(errors.New(\"results truncated due to limit\"))\n\t\t\treturn apiFuncResult{metrics, nil, warnings, closer}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tif set.Err() != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, returnAPIError(set.Err()), warnings, closer}\n\t}\n\n\treturn apiFuncResult{metrics, nil, warnings, closer}\n}\n\nfunc (*API) dropSeries(*http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorInternal, errors.New(\"not implemented\")}, nil, nil}\n}\n\n// Target has the information for one target.\ntype Target struct {\n\t// Labels before any processing.\n\tDiscoveredLabels labels.Labels `json:\"discoveredLabels\"`\n\t// Any labels that are added to this target and its metrics.\n\tLabels labels.Labels `json:\"labels\"`\n\n\tScrapePool string `json:\"scrapePool\"`\n\tScrapeURL  string `json:\"scrapeUrl\"`\n\tGlobalURL  string `json:\"globalUrl\"`\n\n\tLastError          string              `json:\"lastError\"`\n\tLastScrape         time.Time           `json:\"lastScrape\"`\n\tLastScrapeDuration float64             `json:\"lastScrapeDuration\"`\n\tHealth             scrape.TargetHealth `json:\"health\"`\n\n\tScrapeInterval string `json:\"scrapeInterval\"`\n\tScrapeTimeout  string `json:\"scrapeTimeout\"`\n}\n\ntype ScrapePoolsDiscovery struct {\n\tScrapePools []string `json:\"scrapePools\"`\n}\n\n// DroppedTarget has the information for one target that was dropped during relabelling.\ntype DroppedTarget struct {\n\t// Labels before any processing.\n\tDiscoveredLabels labels.Labels `json:\"discoveredLabels\"`\n\tScrapePool       string        `json:\"scrapePool\"`\n}\n\n// TargetDiscovery has all the active targets.\ntype TargetDiscovery struct {\n\tActiveTargets       []*Target        `json:\"activeTargets\"`\n\tDroppedTargets      []*DroppedTarget `json:\"droppedTargets\"`\n\tDroppedTargetCounts map[string]int   `json:\"droppedTargetCounts\"`\n}\n\n// GlobalURLOptions contains fields used for deriving the global URL for local targets.\ntype GlobalURLOptions struct {\n\tListenAddress string\n\tHost          string\n\tScheme        string\n}\n\n// sanitizeSplitHostPort acts like net.SplitHostPort.\n// Additionally, if there is no port in the host passed as input, we return the\n// original host, making sure that IPv6 addresses are not surrounded by square\n// brackets.\nfunc sanitizeSplitHostPort(input string) (string, string, error) {\n\thost, port, err := net.SplitHostPort(input)\n\tif err != nil && strings.HasSuffix(err.Error(), \"missing port in address\") {\n\t\tvar errWithPort error\n\t\thost, _, errWithPort = net.SplitHostPort(input + \":80\")\n\t\tif errWithPort == nil {\n\t\t\terr = nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn host, port, err\n}\n\nfunc getGlobalURL(u *url.URL, opts GlobalURLOptions) (*url.URL, error) {\n\thost, port, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(u.Host)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn u, err\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, lhr := range LocalhostRepresentations {\n\t\tif host == lhr {\n\t\t\t_, ownPort, err := net.SplitHostPort(opts.ListenAddress)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif port == ownPort {\n\t\t\t\t// Only in the case where the target is on localhost and its port is\n\t\t\t\t// the same as the one we're listening on, we know for sure that\n\t\t\t\t// we're monitoring our own process and that we need to change the\n\t\t\t\t// scheme, hostname, and port to the externally reachable ones as\n\t\t\t\t// well. We shouldn't need to touch the path at all, since if a\n\t\t\t\t// path prefix is defined, the path under which we scrape ourselves\n\t\t\t\t// should already contain the prefix.\n\t\t\t\tu.Scheme = opts.Scheme\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = opts.Host\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t// Otherwise, we only know that localhost is not reachable\n\t\t\t\t// externally, so we replace only the hostname by the one in the\n\t\t\t\t// external URL. It could be the wrong hostname for the service on\n\t\t\t\t// this port, but it's still the best possible guess.\n\t\t\t\thost, _, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(opts.Host)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = host\n\t\t\t\tif port != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\t\tu.Host = net.JoinHostPort(u.Host, port)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn u, nil\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) scrapePools(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tnames := api.scrapePoolsRetriever(r.Context()).ScrapePools()\n\tsort.Strings(names)\n\tres := &ScrapePoolsDiscovery{ScrapePools: names}\n\treturn apiFuncResult{data: res, err: nil, warnings: nil, finalizer: nil}\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) targets(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tgetSortedPools := func(targets map[string][]*scrape.Target) ([]string, int) {\n\t\tvar n int\n\t\tpools := make([]string, 0, len(targets))\n\t\tfor p, t := range targets {\n\t\t\tpools = append(pools, p)\n\t\t\tn += len(t)\n\t\t}\n\t\tslices.Sort(pools)\n\t\treturn pools, n\n\t}\n\n\tscrapePool := r.URL.Query().Get(\"scrapePool\")\n\tstate := strings.ToLower(r.URL.Query().Get(\"state\"))\n\tshowActive := state ==   globalURL.String(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastError: func() string {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tswitch {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tcase err == nil && lastErrStr == \"\":\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\treturn \"\"\n\t\t\t\t\t\tcase err != rules(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tif err := r.ParseForm(); err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf(\"error parsing form values: %w\", err)}, nil, struct{}{}\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn set\n\t}\n\n\trnSet := queryFormToSet(r.Form[\"rule_name[]\"])\n\trgSet := queryFormToSet(r.Form[\"rule_group[]\"])\n\tfSet := {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"exclude_alerts\")\n\t}\n\n\tmaxGroups, nextToken, parseErr := parseListRulesPaginationRequest(r)\n\tif parseErr != nil {\n\t\treturn *parseErr\n\t}\n\n\trgs := getRuleGroupNextToken(grp.File(), grp.Name()) {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tfoundToken = true\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif len(rgSet) > 0 {\n\t\t\tif _, ok := rgSet[grp.Name()]; !ok {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif len(fSet) > 0 {\n\t\t\tif _, ok := fSet[grp.File()]; !ok {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tapiRuleGroup := &RuleGroup{\n\t\t\tName:           grp.Name(),\n\t\t\tFile:           grp.File(),\n\t\t\tInterval:       grp.Interval().Seconds(),\n\t\t\tLimit:          grp.Limit(),\n\t\t\tRules:          []Rule{},\n\t\t\tEvaluationTime: grp.GetEvaluationTime().Seconds(),\n\t\t\tLastEvaluation: grp.GetLastEvaluation(),\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfor _, rr := range grp.Rules(matcherSets...) {\n\t\t\tvar enrichedRule Rule\n\n\t\t\tif len(rnSet) > 0 rr.LastError().Error()\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tswitch rule := rr.(type) {\n\t\t\tcase *rules.AlertingRule:\n\t\t\t\tif !returnAlerts {\n\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tvar activeAlerts     \"alerting\",\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tcase *rules.RecordingRule:\n\t\t\t\tif !returnRecording {\n\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tenrichedRule = RecordingRule{\n\t\t\t\t\tName: \"recording\",\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\terr := fmt.Errorf(\"failed to assert type of rule '%v'\", rule.Name())\n\t\t\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorInternal, err}, nil, nil}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif enrichedRule != nil {\n\t\t\t\tapiRuleGroup.Rules = append(apiRuleGroup.Rules, enrichedRule)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// If the rule group response has no rules, skip it - this one. Therefore a next token is required.\n\t\t\t\tres.GroupNextToken = getRuleGroupNextToken(grp.File(), grp.Name())\n\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\trgs = append(rgs, apiRuleGroup)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif maxGroups > 0 && nextToken != \"\" && !foundToken {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(fmt.Errorf(\"invalid group_next_token '%v'. were rule groups changed?\", nextToken), \"group_next_token\")\n\t}\n\n\tres.RuleGroups = rgs\n\treturn apiFuncResult{res, nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\nfunc parseExcludeAlerts(r *http.Request) (bool, error) {\n\texcludeAlertsParam := string is needed to get the position information for the annotations, and it\n// can be empty if the position information isn't needed.\nfunc (api *API) respond(w http.ResponseWriter, req *http.Request, data any, warnings annotations.Annotations, query string) {\n\tstatusMessage := statusSuccess\n\twarn, info := warnings.AsStrings(query, 10, 10)\n\n\tresp := &Response{\n\t\tStatus:   statusMessage,\n\t\tData:     data,\n\t\tWarnings: warn,\n\t\tInfos:    info,\n\t}\n\n\tcodec, err := api.negotiateCodec(req, resp)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tapi.respondError(w, &apiError{errorNotAcceptable, err}, nil)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tb, err := codec.Encode(resp)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tapi.logger.Error(\"error marshaling response\", \"url\", req.URL, \"err\", err)\n\t\thttp.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", codec.ContentType().String())\n\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\tif n, err := w.Write(b); err != nil {\n\t\tapi.logger.Error(\"error writing response\", \"url\", req.URL, \"bytesWritten\", n, \"err\", err)\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) negotiateCodec(req *http.Request, resp *Response) (Codec, error) {\n\tfor _, clause := range goautoneg.ParseAccept(req.Header.Get(\"Accept\")) {\n\t\tfor _, codec := range api.codecs {\n\t\t\tif codec.ContentType().Satisfies(clause) && codec.CanEncode(resp) {\n\t\t\t\treturn codec, nil\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tdefaultCodec := api.codecs[0]\n\tif !defaultCodec.CanEncode(resp) {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"cannot encode response as %s\", defaultCodec.ContentType())\n\t}\n\n\treturn defaultCodec, nil\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) respondError(w http.ResponseWriter, apiErr *apiError, data any) {\n\tjson := jsoniter.ConfigCompatibleWithStandardLibrary\n\tb, err := json.Marshal(&Response{\n\t\tStatus:    statusError,\n\t\tErrorType: apiErr.typ.str,\n\t\tError:     apiErr.err.Error(),\n\t\tData:      data,\n\t})\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tapi.logger.Error(\"error marshaling json response\", \"err\", err)\n\t\thttp.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tvar code errorBadData:\n\t\treturn http.StatusBadRequest\n\tcase errorExec:\n\t\treturn http.StatusUnprocessableEntity\n\tcase errorCanceled:\n\t\treturn statusClientClosedConnection\n\tcase errorTimeout:\n\t\treturn http.StatusServiceUnavailable\n\tcase errorInternal:\n\t\treturn http.StatusInternalServerError\n\tcase errorNotFound:\n\t\treturn http.StatusNotFound\n\tcase errorNotAcceptable:\n\t\treturn http.StatusNotAcceptable\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn http.StatusInternalServerError\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc parseTimeParam(r *http.Request, paramName string, defaultValue time.Time) (time.Time, error) {\n\tval := r.FormValue(paramName)\n\tif val == \"\" {\n\t\treturn defaultValue, nil\n\t}\n\tresult, err := parseTime(val)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn time.Time{}, fmt.Errorf(\"invalid time value for '%s': %w\", paramName, err)\n\t}\n\treturn result, nil\n}\n\nfunc parseTime(s string) (time.Time, error) {\n\tif t, err := strconv.ParseFloat(s, 64); err == nil {\n\t\ts, ns := math.Modf(t)\n\t\tns = math.Round(ns*1000) / 1000\n\t\treturn time.Unix(int64(s), int64(ns*float64(time.Second))).UTC(), nil\n\t}\n\tif t, err := time.Parse(time.RFC3339Nano, s); err == nil {\n\t\treturn t, nil\n\t}\n\n\t// Stdlib's time parser can only handle 4 digit years. As a workaround until\n\t// that is fixed we want to at least support our own boundary times.\n\t// Context: https://github.com/prometheus/client_golang/issues/614\n\t// Upstream issue: https://github.com/golang/go/issues/20555\n\tswitch s {\n\tcase minTimeFormatted:\n\t\treturn MinTime, nil\n\tcase maxTimeFormatted:\n\t\treturn MaxTime, nil\n\t}\n\treturn time.Time{}, fmt.Errorf(\"cannot parse %q to a valid timestamp\", s)\n}\n\nfunc parseDuration(s string) (time.Duration, error) {\n\tif d, err := strconv.ParseFloat(s, 64); err == nil {\n\t\tts := d * float64(time.Second)\n\t\tif ts > float64(math.MaxInt64) || ts < float64(math.MinInt64) {\n\t\t\treturn 0, fmt.Errorf(\"cannot parse %q to a valid duration. It overflows int64\", s)\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn time.Duration(ts), nil\n\t}\n\tif d, err := model.ParseDuration(s); err == nil {\n\t\treturn time.Duration(d), nil\n\t}\n\treturn 0, fmt.Errorf(\"cannot parse %q to a valid duration\", s)\n}\n\nfunc parseMatchersParam(matchers []string) ([][]*labels.Matcher, error) {\n\tmatcherSets, err := parser.ParseMetricSelectors(matchers)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\nOUTER:\n\tfor _, ms := range matcherSets {\n\t\tfor _, lm := range ms {\n\t\t\tif lm != nil && !lm.Matches(\"\") {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue OUTER\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn nil, errors.New(\"match[] must contain at least one non-empty matcher\")\n\t}\n\treturn matcherSets, nil\n}\n\n// parseLimitParam returning 0 means no limit is to be applied.\nfunc parseLimitParam(limitStr string) (limit int, err error) {\n\tif limitStr == \"\" {\n\t\treturn limit, nil\n\t}\n\n\tlimit, err = strconv.Atoi(limitStr)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn limit, err\n\t}\n\tif limit < 0 {\n\t\treturn limit, errors.New(\"limit must be non-negative\")\n\t}\n\n\treturn limit, nil\n}\n\n// toHintLimit increases the API limit, as returned by parseLimitParam, by 1.\n// This allows for emitting warnings when the results are truncated.\nfunc toHintLimit(limit int) int {\n\t// 0 means no limit and avoid int overflow\n\tif limit > 0 && limit < math.MaxInt {\n\t\treturn limit + 1\n\t}\n\treturn limit\n}\n\n// truncateResults truncates result for queryRange() and query().\n// No truncation for other types(Scalars or Strings).\nfunc truncateResults(result *promql.Result, limit int) (*promql.Result, bool) {\n\tisTruncated := false\n\n\tswitch v := result.Value.(type) {\n\tcase promql.Matrix:\n\t\tif len(v) > limit {\n\t\t\tresult.Value = v[:limit]\n\t\t\tisTruncated = true\n\t\t}\n\tcase promql.Vector:\n\t\tif len(v) > limit {\n\t\t\tresult.Value = v[:limit]\n\t\t\tisTruncated = true\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Return the modified result. Unchanged for other types.\n\treturn result, isTruncated\n}\n",

package v1

import (
	"context"
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"
	"net/http"
	"time"
)

// SilenceMatcher represents a single label matcher in a silence.
type SilenceMatcher struct {
	Name    string `json:"name"`
	Value   string `json:"value"`
	IsRegex bool   `json:"isRegex"`
	IsEqual bool   `json:"isEqual"`
}

// Silence represents an alertmanager silence definition.
type Silence struct {
	ID        string           `json:"id,omitempty"`
	Matchers  []SilenceMatcher `json:"matchers"`
	StartsAt  time.Time        `json:"startsAt"`
	EndsAt    time.Time        `json:"endsAt"`
	CreatedBy string           `json:"createdBy"`
	Comment   string           `json:"comment"`
}

// SilenceManager defines the interface for creating and managing silences.
type SilenceManager interface {
	CreateSilence(ctx context.Context, s Silence) (string, error)
}

func validateSilence(s Silence) error {
	if len(s.Matchers) == 0 {
		return fmt.Errorf("silence must have at least one matcher")
	}
	for _, m := range s.Matchers {
		if m.Name == "" {
			return fmt.Errorf("matcher name must not be empty")
		}
	}
	if s.StartsAt.IsZero() {
		return fmt.Errorf("startsAt must be set")
	}
	if s.EndsAt.IsZero() {
		return fmt.Errorf("
... (truncated)

package v1

import (
	"bytes"
	"context"
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"
	"net/http"
	"net/http/httptest"
	"testing"
	"time"

	"github.com/stretchr/testify/require"
)

// mockSilenceManager is a test double for SilenceManager.
type mockSilenceManager struct {
	createFn func(ctx context.Context, s Silence) (string, error)
	counter  int
}

func (m *mockSilenceManager) CreateSilence(ctx context.Context, s Silence) (string, error) {
	if m.createFn != nil {
		return m.createFn(ctx, s)
	}
	m.counter++
	return fmt.Sprintf("silence-%d", m.counter), nil
}

// validTestSilence returns a Silence that passes all validation checks.
func validTestSilence(n int) Silence {
	now := time.Now()
	return Silence{
		Matchers: []SilenceMatcher{
			{Name: "alertname", Value: fmt.Sprintf("TestAlert%d", n), IsEqual: true},
		},
		StartsAt:  now,
		EndsAt:    now.Add(time.Hour),
		CreatedBy: "testuser",
		Comment:   fmt.Sprintf("test silence %d", n),
	}
}
